Shen Bao Second Sheet

A Major Key to Peace in Central Europe: France and Italy Reach Complete Compromise

Four Documents to be Signed Soon

African Issues Also Resolved

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval continued their discussions last night. They have reached complete agreement on all issues, including Italy's request for land in North Africa. Both politicians attended the banquet of the French ambassador at the French embassy last night. After the banquet, they retired to a private room and discussed until nearly midnight. When Laval left the embassy and returned to his hotel, he looked tired but happy, and told the waiting journalists, ["We can sign tomorrow"]. Now there are four documents that will be signed by Mussolini representing Italy and Laval representing France: (1) A statement recording the same opinions of France and Italy on major issues of general policy. (2) A document jointly inviting the neighboring countries and successor countries of the former Austro-Hungarian Empire to conclude a convention on their borders and non-interference. (3) A consultation convention between France and Italy stipulating that the two countries shall assume mutual consultation to deal with matters when the independence of Austria is endangered, and will invite Germany, Hungary, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, Poland, and Romania to join the treaty. (4) A convention dealing with the North African colonial issues between France and Italy. It is expected that the first document will be published soon, and the rest will be published later or at the same time as the protocol reconciling certain special issues of diplomatic policy between France and Italy. (7th Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) The Franco-Italian negotiations have been officially announced, and an agreement has been reached. The new agreement will be published tonight after the representatives of the two countries formally sign it. According to the first person to receive the news of the agreement, it was the French veterans, because at the French embassy banquet last night, representatives of French veterans were also invited to attend. After the banquet, Mussolini and Laval entered another room to confer. Not long after, they returned to the lobby of the embassy. Laval then introduced the representatives of the French and Italian veterans to Mussolini. At that time, Laval announced that France and Italy had reached a new agreement. (7th Havas Telegram)

Franco-Italian African Issues

(Rome) Italian Premier Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval held talks for three hours yesterday afternoon, and then issued a half-official statement, mainly stating that France and Italy had reached a proper agreement on a pact to guarantee Austria's independence. However, opinions on colonial affairs in Africa were still not in agreement. The two statesmen are now vigorously arguing about ceding African territory to Italy. In the past two days, each has been assisted by experts in African affairs to address this issue with a friendly and determined attitude. Italy's demands are based on the promises of land concessions made by Britain and France to Italy when it joined the Great War in 1915. The colonial issues between France and Italy can be divided into the following four categories:

(1) How many generations of Italian nationals in Tunis should be allowed to retain their nationality?

(2) Regarding the land south of Italian Libya, Italy wants the land south of Tibesti Maya. France proposed that the land obtained by Italy should be limited to the area north of that region, fearing that French West Africa and French Equatorial Africa would be cut off.

(3) Italy is now demanding 50 miles of Somaliland, which currently belongs to France.

(4) Italy wants more than 2,000 shares of the Addis Ababa Railway that France has agreed to give to Italy. At the same time, according to Reuters Berlin, the details of the discussions between France and Italy in Rome will be announced to the German Foreign Ministry by the French and Italian ambassadors in Berlin today or tomorrow. Last week, the French ambassador went to the German Foreign Ministry several times to inform the German government of the progress of the negotiations. According to German political circles, they have not received any definite information on the conditions of any new pact proposals. Berlin newspapers comment on the Rome conference with considerable indifference. Germany seems to be trying to delay the matter to give itself time to thoroughly consider its position before expressing its views. (Reuters, 7th)

(Rome) Today is the second day of French Foreign Minister Laval's visit to Rome. Regarding the results of today's Franco-Italian talks, although the two governments have not yet reached a final agreement, the negotiations can be said to have made important new progress. Among them, the draft pact on maintaining Austria's independence and developing the economy of the Danube River basin has been agreed upon in principle. As for the draft agreement on coordinating the resolution of Franco-Italian disputes in Africa, experts are working hard to reach a compromise between the two countries. It is heard that Italy has accepted the gradual abandonment of the special interests enjoyed by Italian nationals in French Tunisia under the Franco-Italian Treaty of 1896. The deadline for the abandonment has not yet been determined, but it will be no later than 1965. In return for this concession by Italy, France agrees to amend the 1916 agreement on North African colonies. France agrees to cede territory south of Italian Libya along the Tibesti Mountains, but the port of Lake Chad is not included. In Somaliland, France is prepared to revise the border, extend the border of Italian Eritrea, and allow Italy to participate in the operation of the French Djibouti Railway for the export of Abyssinian goods. Although this issue is quite complicated, it is still not difficult to obtain a fair, appropriate, and mutually beneficial solution. Therefore, both France and Italy now hope that the final agreement can be signed tomorrow. After the above four documents are formally signed, the first document, namely the Franco-Italian record of talks, will be sent to the newspapers for publication. However, the remaining three documents will be announced separately in the future. In addition, protocols may be signed stipulating that the governments of France and Italy adopt a coordinated attitude on certain special issues of foreign policy. (Havas, 6th)

Content of Franco-Italian Agreement

(Rome) The wording of the Franco-Italian agreement is now being finalized by representatives of the two countries. The work will continue until morning, and it is expected that the signing will not take place until midday. There are four types of documents in this agreement, which differ slightly from what was transmitted in the previous cable:

(1) An official communique stating that the two governments share harmonious views on major issues related to African colonial affairs and general politics.

(2) A record of the talks between France and Italy, in which the two countries promise to consult each other when Austria's independence is threatened, and to suggest to Austria's neighboring countries and the successor states of the Austro-Hungarian Empire the signing of a pact recognizing mutual respect for existing borders and non-interference in the internal affairs of other signatory countries.

(3) Three draft colonial pacts: (A) Resolving the issue of the status of Italian nationals in French Tunisia. Italy will abandon the special interests enjoyed by Italian nationals under the Franco-Italian Treaty of 1896 in 1965. (B) and (C) Stipulate the territorial concessions made by France in Italian Libya and Somaliland.

(4) Protocol: In this protocol, France and Italy interpret the Five-Power Declaration and agree to declare that if Germany does not conclude a special agreement with the major powers one day, the issue of German rearmament will continue to be open for discussion at any time. The wording of the above documents is temporarily kept secret, but the main points will be explained by Laval and Mussolini in a statement to the press tonight. (Havas, 7th)

Grand Banquet in Rome

(Rome) Last night, the French Embassy in Villa Farnese held a grand banquet, opening a new chapter in the history of Franco-Italian relations. This was only the fourth time that Italian Premier Mussolini had personally visited the embassy to attend a banquet. The previous three visits were merely of a diplomatic nature. Last night, the embassy gate was brightly lit by electric torches, illuminating it as if it were daytime. All the windows were decorated with lights in the Roman style. The Galara Gallery in the embassy is a famous building, and the banquet was held there. Guests gathered together, including two famous generals who had won the highest medals in Italy, in addition to Italian Prime Minister and French Foreign Minister Laval: General Bartoglio and Naval Admiral Teon di Laval. Other dignitaries included Undersecretaries Suvich and Lassoni, former Italian ambassadors to France Avanzana, Naxi, and Mansoni, followed by Count Volpi, Baron Aloisi, and key figures from the Italian Foreign Ministry who participated in the Franco-Italian talks. Cabinet ministers and prominent figures from Roman society also participated in the grand event. (Havas, 6th)

Germany Indifferent, Austria Satisfied

(London) According to a Reuters dispatch from Berlin, the German government is now adopting a reserved attitude towards the Franco-Italian agreement, because Germany must carefully study this pact before it can decide whether to participate or not. (Reuters, 7th)

(Berlin) Regarding the negotiations between France and Italy in Rome, German political circles maintain an extremely reserved attitude, and newspapers have not issued any clear comments, presumably due to instructions from the authorities. (Havas, 6th)

This declaration contained the intention of the three countries to prepare to consult when necessary, so Britain's position has already been clarified. Many believe that Britain does not need to issue another declaration now. It is heard that the governments of France and Italy are now satisfied with the British government's position on this matter. Interpretation of Eligibility for Committee Members of Trade Associations

(Nanjing) The Central People's Movement Committee requested the Judicial Yuan to interpret the eligibility of committee members of trade associations. The answer is as follows: Committee members are selected from representatives of members. Therefore, if the store that originally dispatched the representative has closed down, or if the representative himself has completely separated from the association's business, according to Article 4 of Item 2 of the revised Guidelines for Guiding People's Movement (the constituent members of people's organizations should be based on the principle of prohibiting those who are not currently engaged in the profession from participating), their eligibility as committee members should naturally be lost. If the representative himself leaves the store that originally dispatched him, he has lost the basis for his dispatch, and his original eligibility cannot continue to exist. If, after leaving, he serves in another store that has joined the association, even if the store re-nominates him as a representative, his old eligibility has already been lost, and if he has not been nominated, there is no need to discuss it. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

President Wang's New Work

Distributed to Authorities of Various Countries

(Nanjing) The recent work of Executive Yuan President Wang Zhaoming, "China's Problems and Their Solutions," describes China's political, industrial, commercial, economic, and social conditions, as well as various construction facilities. In addition to the Chinese version, the book also has English, German, and French versions. Wang personally signed the copies and distributed one copy each to the Prime Ministers and Foreign Ministers of various countries. They will be mailed to embassies abroad for distribution. The Chargé d'Affaires of the various countries stationed in China will also be given a copy by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs so that they may have a clear understanding of our policy. The original Chinese version of the book has been sent to the ambassadors and ministers stationed abroad, and a copy has also been distributed to the heads of various Yuan, ministries, and committees, as well as the chairmen of provincial governments. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

Silver House Robbed in Tianjin Japanese Concession

Two Robbers Captured

(Tianjin) At 1:30 PM today, two robbers broke into the Shisheng Silver House on Simianlan Street in the Tianjin Japanese Concession. One was armed with a gun and the other with a knife. When the doorman tried to stop them, the robber with the knife cut his ear and forced the people in the house to retreat to the backyard. Because the cashier was slightly late, he was cut in the face by the robber. The two robbers stole more than 2,000 yuan in cash from the counter and 1,000 yuan in gold unit tickets used by the customs and fled towards Songdao Street and Dunrong Street. When the people in the house escaped through the back door and shouted for help, the Japanese police fired shots in pursuit. The robber with the knife fell behind and was captured. The robber with the gun fought and fled, throwing the stolen cash into the garden in front of the building. The police from No. 72 in front of the building saw this, drew their guns, and prepared to shoot. The robber stumbled in fear and was captured. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

Fujian Paper Industry Declines

(Fuzhou) The paper produced in various counties in northwestern Fujian used to be sold to the northeast. Recently, due to the establishment of customs by the puppet organization to collect import taxes, and Japanese paper mills in Dalian competing for sales, sales have decreased day by day. The price has fallen from four yuan to two yuan, but it is still difficult to maintain. Many paper dealers in Fuzhou have accumulated a large amount of inventory and have stopped operating one after another. Factories in the production areas have reduced their scope, and many workers have lost their jobs. (Central News Agency, 7th)

Philippines Restricts Retailers

(Xiamen) The Philippine retail restriction bill has been passed by the Philippine Executive Yuan. It will take effect upon passage by the Senate and approval by the Philippine Governor. The main idea is that foreign retailers are not allowed to operate retail businesses. Existing foreign retailers must be terminated before December 31, 1936. For joint ventures, at least 75% of the shares must be held by American and Filipino citizens. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

Bengbu Banks' Profits Last Year

(Bengbu) The profits of various banks in Bengbu in 1934 were as follows: China 85,000 yuan, Shanghai more than 80,000 yuan, Transportation 60,000 yuan, Jiangsu 10,000 yuan, China Industrial 3,000 yuan. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

Japanese Business in Wuhu Plans to Lease Land to Build Wharf

Special Commissioner Telegraphed Provincial Government and Foreign Ministry for Instructions; Local Landowners from Jiangxi Vow to Oppose to the Death

Wuhu Correspondence: Since the Opium War and the signing of the Treaty of Nanjing, Wuhu has been opened as one of the commercial ports along the Yangtze River. Foreign shipping companies have been able to dock at Wuhu to transport goods and passengers. The impact on our shipping rights and commerce has been enormous. Jardine Matheson, Swire, and other companies have successively leased land along the riverbank to set up lighters and wharves. Their business is far more prosperous than our only China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company spared no effort to set up a barge dock upstream of the Jardine Matheson Wharf two years ago, which made it slightly more convenient for passengers to get on and off the ship. Japanese ships have also been sailing between Shanghai and Hankou for a long time. However, in Wuhu, apart from setting up the Osaka barge in the middle of the river, they have not had a wharf on the riverbank due to the lack of an address. However, for the sake of business competition, the desire to find land and develop a wharf has never been forgotten. A Japanese company once planned to purchase the Jiang'an riverbank for 150,000 yuan for the purpose of building a wharf, but the land rights belonged to fellow Jiangxi natives living in Wuhu. The people of Jiangxi, deeply aware of the importance of national sovereignty and understanding the general righteousness, refused to accept the offer, and the matter was suspended. Recently, seeing that the commercial ships of various companies on the Yangtze River have wharves and barge docks, which are much more convenient for travelers to get on and off the ship than using small boats, and that there is no possibility of winning the competition in terms of business, they again stirred up the Japanese Consul in Wuhu, Yoshiharu Kichi, to write to the Wuhu Second District Special Commissioner's Office, proposing to build a bridge on the Linjiang beach first, so that the riverbank can directly reach the barge, and re-submitted the previous proposal to lease land to build a wharf, and repeatedly met to discuss, expressing that it must achieve its purpose. Currently, Special Commissioner Wang Baoqi has telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government and the Nanjing Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions. At the same time, the Jiangxi people living in Wuhu believe that the land is their property and that the Chinese people have an obligation to protect the shipping rights and land rights of the motherland. They have vowed to oppose this to the end and will never lose an inch of land to be seized by others. They have organized a committee to protect the land and shipping and vow to oppose it to the death. (6th)

Respect for the Elderly Meeting Held in Taiyuan

Two Hundred Elders Participate in the Grand Event; Ninety-Three-Year-Old Man Leads in Singing

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Provincial Public Education Center invited the elderly over seventy years old in Taiyuan to hold a respect for the elderly meeting at the center on New Year's Day this year. Zhao Cilong, former Director of the Supervisory Yuan, attended the meeting and gave a speech. More than two hundred elders participated, and more than a thousand people watched, making it a very grand occasion. After the meeting, commemorative badges were issued, and a tea party was held. Here is a record of the proceedings: On that day, Director Wang Gengshen and Deputy Director Ke Dingchu, along with the staff of the center, warmly welcomed the guests on the spot. By 11:00 AM, the participating elders, in groups of three or five, came together. They were all over seventy years old. Although they were old and frail, they were delighted. Most of them were accompanied by their children and grandchildren, with white hair and young faces reflecting each other, creating a picturesque scene. The respect for the elderly meeting was held in the auditorium of the Public Education Center. National flags were crossed in front of the door, and slogans were posted on both sides. Inside the hall was a plaque with the words "[Meeting with Elderly Heroes]." The seats for the elderly were in the middle, and the sides were for male and female guests to visit. At the beginning of the meeting, Chairman Wang Gengshen presided over the meeting and performed the rituals. Then, Zhao Cilong was invited to give a speech, in which he praised the elders, and brought printed copies of "He Ding Jian" (recorded from the Surangama Sutra) to distribute on the spot. After the speech, he shouted "Amitabha" three times, and the whole audience echoed him, as if they were in a meditation hall. Zhao's devotion to Buddhism can be seen from this. Then, the famous painter and calligrapher Chang Zanchun lectured on the system of respecting the elderly in the past. Then, the ninety-three-year-old Wang Fuji was invited to report on his life and sing a "Waking the World Song" once. His tone was clear and bright, not diminished by age, proving that he usually knew how to maintain his health and was not declining in old age. The next speaker after Wang was the seventy-five-year-old Su Jiwen, whose words were humorous and relaxed, creating a lot of fun. Then, Ke Dingchu gave a reply. Finally, commemorative badges were distributed, and after photography and refreshments, the staff of the center led the elders to visit all the exhibition halls of the center, and showed movies in the center's public cinema and played music in the auditorium to entertain the elders. Wang Fuji, the ninety-three-year-old man attending the meeting, and Chang Zanchun, the painter and calligrapher, both immediately wrote inscriptions to commemorate the event. (2nd)

International Commercial Telegrams

丨Reuters Special Business Report, January 7丨

Gold and Silver

British Gold: The London gold price today was 142 shillings and 1 pence, up 5 and a half pence.

British Silver: The London silver market fell 1.25, with the spot price at 24 pence and 5625/10000, and the futures price at 24 pence and 6875/10000. China and India sold, while the United States and speculators bought. The close was stable.

American Silver: The Mountrie silver market was stagnant, and prices did not change much.

Indian Silver: The Bombay silver market trended downwards, and the close was calm. The spot price was 65 rupees and 3 annas, down 4 annas.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market saw good trading this morning, with the pound sterling being heavily sold. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to US dollars was $4.92125, which was 0.25 lower than the closing rate on Saturday and Sunday. The pound sterling fell sharply before noon, with the latest price at $4.913125, down 0.008125 from the opening price. Additionally, one US dollar was equivalent to four shillings and 0.849 pence.

British-French: The opening price was 74.21 francs, a rebound of six points from 2:00 PM on Saturday and Sunday, to 74.15 francs.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market, the pound was weak, opening at $4.91375, which was 0.01 lower than the closing price on Saturday and Sunday. However, the pound remained stable after the opening.

American-French: The opening exchange rate was $6.62375, down 0.00125.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: Cotton market opened this morning with very light trading, as everyone awaited the release of the budget proposal. Overseas cotton prices were slightly lower, prompting long position liquidation, but it was absorbed by dealers. Opening prices were slightly lower, but later due to purchases by dealers and spot traders...

Indian Cotton: In the Bombay cotton market, purchases by bullish operators absorbed sales from brokers and retail investors. The price of White American cotton for April/May delivery was 238.5 rupees, an increase of 1 rupee.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was calm today. At 1:00 PM, the price for March delivery fell by three points, to 687.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market had better sentiment this morning. At 1:00 PM, the price for May delivery was 5 shillings and 2.25 pence, which was 0.375 higher than Saturday and Sunday.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened strong and stable, with an upward trend. Wheat and coarse grains were both up by a strong half-cent, due to good sentiment in the European wheat market and increased demand for fodder due to the cold weather in the United States.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was calm today. At noon, the transaction price for April/May delivery was 6.8125 pence, 0.0625 lower than on Saturday and Sunday.

Securities

New York: Before the opening of the New York stock market, favorable factors included news from "Steel" magazine that steel mills' operations last week reached 42.5% of their production capacity, an increase of 3.5% compared to the previous week. Unfavorable factors included the continued cautious trend in securities trading until President Roosevelt's budget proposal was released. After the market opened this morning, trading was active and stable, with most stocks showing slight gains. As the budget proposal will be released at noon, prices may not show a clear trend before then. According to the Railway Economics Bureau's report this morning, the net operating income of first-class railways in the United States reached $423,118,000 in the eleven months ending in late November, a decrease of $13,368,000 compared to the same period last year. Songjiang

Robbery and Assault Outside the East Gate

Wu Weiyuan, a resident of Xinbang in the 18th Tu outside the East Gate of this city, and his two brothers, the eldest of whom runs the Yongsheng Rice Store in Guozilong, were attacked at about 12 o'clock last night (the 6th) by more than a dozen robbers speaking Jiangbei and local dialects. The robbers jumped in over the outer fence of the Wu family, calling out the victim's name and ordering everyone not to look at them. The robbers were all wearing blue-black short coats and armed with box cannons and Browning guns. They forbade anyone from making noise and carried out a reckless search. Wu Weiyuan's brother was beaten and tied up by the robbers with wooden objects, leaving him covered in injuries. The robbers searched for about an hour before fleeing with their loot. Upon inspection, they found that cash, gold jewelry, pearls, jade, and antiques had been stolen, especially from the two rooms occupied by the newly married couple. Because the bride had returned to Ningbo, the losses could not be calculated. The injured victim has been sent to the Yinhang Hospital for treatment, and the incident has been reported to the relevant Fourth Public Security Substation for investigation and pursuit of the stolen goods. Xinbang is close to Song City, and this major robbery has made residents uneasy.

Suzhou

Robbery and Assault in the City

Wen Muxian, a rice dealer at the Zhaoyuan Rice Store outside Fengmen, was delivering rice to Xie Yaqian and the Yu Chang Rice Store in front of the North Temple on the 6th. Along the way, he collected 156.695 yuan in rice payments. It was already 6:30 PM when he returned. As he was walking near the Nanshuixian Alley in front of the Shuixian Temple in the Cucumber Lane intersection, three burly men suddenly came up from behind and used a sack to cover his head. They then dragged him to a secluded place, used the hemp rope from his rice bag to tie his feet, and then used a sharp blade to slash his forehead. They then stabbed him twice in the thigh, each about an inch deep. They took all the rice payments from his person and fled without a trace. Zhou was injured and fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. A passerby noticed him and reported the incident, and he was sent to Zhuanxi Hospital by police car. A search for the robbers is underway, but as of the afternoon of the 7th, nothing has been found.

Joint Military and Police Parade

County Magistrate Wu Qiyun, in order to strengthen the defense of the city and unify command, organized a winter defense committee, appointing officers from the military, police, business groups, and security teams as members. It is now scheduled to hold the first joint parade of the military, police, business groups, and security teams in the urban area at the Public Sports Ground at 9:00 AM today (the 8th). County Magistrate Wu will give a speech and hold a defense meeting to maintain local security.

Jiading

Account Collector Robbed on the Way

Zhou Yiyan, manager of the Yuelai Yiwandian in this city, was returning from collecting accounts in Kunshan at 7:00 PM on the afternoon of the 5th. While traveling by rickshaw between Malu and Nanxiang, south of Yandun, three robbers suddenly jumped out from the roadside in the darkness, blocking his way with flashlights and pistols. One of them spoke in a Jiangbei accent, while the other two remained silent. They searched Zhou's entire body for a long time, stealing twelve ten-yuan banknotes from the China Industrial Bank and other miscellaneous coins, totaling 138 yuan. They also took a pocket watch and a seal. After completing the search, the robbers took off Zhou's cotton robe and fled south with their loot.

Changshu

Poor People Surround the County Government

The First District Office here has always distributed relief grain to the poor. Impoverished elderly men and women in the district can go to collect it. Beforehand, the township heads submit reports, and distribution is done by name and number. The distribution date is traditionally the first day of each lunar month, with each person receiving 600 cash. This money relies entirely on income from tea house donations. However, since the implementation of the treasury system, this tax revenue is now collected and deposited by the county government, making withdrawals difficult. Therefore, the relief grain has not been distributed for three months. Yesterday (the 6th) was the scheduled distribution date for the twelfth lunar month. In addition to the copper coins, each person is also given a set of cotton clothes and pants, so even more people went to collect it, reaching a total of

four to five hundred men, women, and children. They surrounded the district office from 7:00 AM to 12:00 PM. The district chief informed them that the tax revenue had been transferred to the county government. The crowd then went to the county government to request the distribution, but they were dispersed by the police. The poor people all returned with tears in their eyes.

Deadline of Three Days to Finish Baojia Work

This county has been ordered to implement the Baojia system. After the county magistrate and others made great efforts to promote it, progress has been very smooth. The second phase of Jia compilation is mostly completed. However, due to recent continuous rain and muddy roads, progress has been hindered. However, according to provincial regulations, the third phase of work should begin this month. The county government, fearing delays, has ordered all district chiefs to complete the second phase of work and produce all Baojia chiefs within three days. The third phase of work should begin on the 10th of this month.

Wuxi

Connecting Jiangsu and Zhejiang to Build a Highway

Jiangsu Province is building a highway that encircles Taihu Lake, linking it to the highway in Zhejiang Province. The section from Wuxi to Yixing in Jiangsu Province has already been completed. The Sujia Highway will also connect to Zhejiang Province at the same time. Only the section from Wuxi to Suzhou has not yet been built. Recently, the SuFu Motor Company invested in building the Sumu Road, deciding to extend the route to Guangfu, which is expected to be completed by mid-March. At the same time, the Construction Department has also decided to build a highway from Wuxi via Wangting to Guangfu, in order to connect to the Guangfu section of the Sumu Road, completely completing the provincial highway encircling Taihu Lake. Construction is being expedited and is scheduled to be fully opened to traffic in March. It will then connect to Zhejiang Province's Jiahu Highway, allowing direct automobile traffic between the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang.

Fire in Houshuyuan Alley

The residence of Sun Zhicheng at No. 25 Houshuyuan Alley in the city, located in the middle of the alley, has a total of three bays. The first two bays are single-story, and the third bay is a two-story building. Apart from a portion used by himself, the rest is rented out. Qian Zixiang's family, in the west of the third bay, recently went down to the countryside to attend a wedding banquet, leaving only the maid Zhu Ma at home to guard the door. At 5:30 PM on the day before yesterday (the 6th), Zhu Ma had just returned to the room from washing the chamber pot outside when she suddenly saw thick smoke and flames billowing from the upstairs. She shouted "Fire!" Various firefighting teams rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm. However, the New County Front River channel was shallow and difficult to draw water from, causing the fire to spread. The teams then turned to Jingshu River to draw water and extinguish the fire. However, the three-bay building had already been completely destroyed, causing losses of over ten thousand yuan. During the firefighting, Tao Quangen, a member of the sixth fire brigade in the central district, fell heavily on the Lihuangni Bridge and was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Yinjiang

Privately Made Poison Pills Sent to the Provincial Court for Trial

Li Ruibao, Li Guozhen, Song Chunxiang and other residents of the West Street of Wuchangjing Town, privately set up an organization, secretly manufactured red pills and potent drugs. On November 16th of last year, at midnight, they were reported to the chamber of commerce by the town's drug resistance committee. Song Qixiang and Shen Yu's wife, Ms. Li, were apprehended along with equipment, poisonous pills and other evidence and sent to the county government. They have been interrogated several times. On the 4th, they were brought back to court for a retrial. Song Qixiang testified that all the items were stored by Li Guozhen and that he had no improper relationship with his cousin Shen Li. After the interrogation, the judge Jiang concluded that the case involved the private production of poison pills, which this court had no jurisdiction to try. A written report will be prepared and sent to the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters for legal handling.

Petition of Representatives of Private Small Motor Vehicles

After the privately operated long-distance bus service was established and a macadam road surface was built, privately operated small motor vehicles were only allowed to operate if they had a motor vehicle business and paid a deposit of 100 yuan. The small motor vehicles were struggling to make a living, so Yang Zhaoxiang and others were elected as representatives and came to the county government from Xicheng on the 5th to petition. Secretary Wu received them and the representatives requested approval to set up a joint office and reduce the deposit. Secretary Wu promised to convey the request to the provincial authorities for review.

Qingjiang

Canal Water Rises Sharply in Winter

After winter, the water in the Li Canal within Huaiyin usually drops, never rises. Therefore, it is inconvenient for Qingzhen ferries to operate in winter and they often have to stop. However, recently, the canal water has not only not dropped, but the water level has risen to over four feet, resulting in a water level of two zhang and one chi in Qingjiang and a water level of four zhang, seven chi, and four cun at the Yunkou Fantou Dam. Also, the water level between Qing'an and Fanduo is over two zhang and six chi. This is unprecedented in the past few years. According to canal workers, this year's situation is special because the Liu Lao Jian Dam was closed last winter, causing all the water from the central canal to flow into Li Canal. Secondly, the Weishan Lake Dam was opened, causing a large amount of lake water to flow into the canal. These are the main reasons.

County Notice Strictly Prohibiting the Small Swords Society

Since the Small Swords Society riots in the territory of the Second District of Huaiyin, which resulted in the burning and killing of Yue Kuan Tianjia's family, the rebels have been secretly gathering and have not dispersed. They have ordered blacksmith shops to rush to produce knives and guns day and night, hoping to launch a reckless uprising. The county government received a report and yesterday issued a joint notice with Commander Cao of the garrison, stating that, according to reports, the Small Swords Society in various parts of the Second District is plotting an uprising and rushing to make broadswords. This is a serious violation of the law. Therefore, this notice is issued to inform the public that they must reflect on their actions as soon as possible. Otherwise, if discovered, they will be arrested and punished severely without leniency.

Nantong

Pacifying the Coastal Areas of Northern Jiangsu

After a large number of coastal bandits in northern Jiangsu were attacked by Chi Yaozong, the third district chief of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police, who led the major teams of Liuhe, Qidong, Nantong, and Yancheng, as well as the provincial security team's mortar team, and the Haijun Minister's Changfeng Shenghu and E three gunboats, the bandits were defeated. Chief Chi Ke is leaving his troops to pacify the sea. Shen himself transferred to Yancheng to pursue and suppress the fleeing bandits.

Jiaxing

Theft from the Bank of China Warehouse

The Jiaxing branch of the Bank of China, at the request of the county chamber of commerce and the advice of the county government, established a warehouse to allow farmers and businesses to mortgage goods for funding. The warehouse was established at the Huili Cocoon Factory site at the Zha Yan bottom of Middle Street. Since its establishment, industry, commerce, and farmers have been able to obtain loans by mortgaging goods, which has been of great benefit. Unexpectedly, the second warehouse was entered by thieves through a hole dug in the back wall in the middle of the night the day before yesterday. Forty-three bags of unpolished rice, totaling twenty-one dan and five dou, were stolen. The theft was discovered the next morning and reported to the Fifth Police Station. The Criminal Investigation Team of the County Public Security Bureau went to investigate and ordered a separate search.

Hangzhou

Prostitute Commits Suicide Over Love Affair

Chen Hua, a prostitute, also known as Hong Guiying, 26 years old, from Shangyu, who works at No. 228 Hangzhou Road, Gongbu, was very popular. Chen had a regular customer named Wang Bingrong, a shop assistant at a cloth store in Qinghefang, who was from Pingyao, Hangzhou County. The two had a very close relationship and had made a lifelong commitment. Wang had not visited Gongbu for two months after losing his job, so Chen suspected that Wang had fallen in love with someone else. She went to Pingyao to visit him and found that Wang did indeed have a wife and children. She immediately swallowed the gold jewelry she was wearing and committed suicide. After being discovered, she was rushed back by car, but she died at Xiaohe. The Hangzhou District Court was notified and sent a prosecutor to examine and prepare the body for burial.

Xiaoshan

Farmer Couple Commits Suicide Due to Crop Failure

Xiaoshan suffered a severe drought last summer and autumn, and the harvest was poor. Farmers in the four townships are unable to make a living in the middle of winter, and there are daily reports of people committing suicide. In Dongwang, in the west of the district, a farmer named Wang Jichen's family of seven, who farmed more than ten mu of land, had no harvest since the drought last summer, and they had no straw for roofing. On the 4th of this month, the landlord demanded the payment of rent, and Wang could not pay, so he hanged himself. His wife, because her husband had already committed suicide, and she was unable to support the family, also drowned herself in the Wenyan Pond on the afternoon of the 5th. She was pulled out of the water, but she had already died.

Hefei

Record of the First Trial Run on the Luohua Section of the Huainan Railway

The Central Construction Committee began construction in the spring of the 23rd year of the Huainan Coal Mine Railway, from Luohe Street to the Erba Dam in Wuhu. It was supervised by Chief Engineer Chen Shifan, with a budget of 8 million yuan. The section from Luohe to Hefei was completed by early last winter. The section between Zhujia Alley, 100 li from Hefei, and Luohe had already been opened to traffic, but two bridges on the way from Zhujia Alley to Hefei had not yet been completed. Chief Engineer Chen had agreed with the Construction Committee that the Luohe section would be opened to traffic by the end of the 23rd year, so after winter, he supervised the workers to speed up construction day and night. Fortunately, the bridges were completed by mid-December. It was decided to open the line to traffic on the 30th. Chen traveled from Luohe to Shanghai by train. After receiving the notice, the Railway Engineering Office in Hefei prepared a welcome in advance and invited various public organizations to visit. However, due to more than ten days of rain, Chen feared that the newly built roadbed was not stable and temporarily suspended the opening on the 30th. He sent employees to inspect the entire section once. On the 31st, Chen departed from Luohe at 8:00 AM, riding on a locomotive pulling eight freight cars, driving slowly to prevent danger. At 12:00 PM, he arrived at Zhujia Alley. After a short stop, he drove east, but carefully inspected the route along the way. He finally arrived at the temporary station outside the east gate at 9:00 PM. The Railway Engineering Office in Hefei set off firecrackers to welcome him. That night, he sent an urgent telegram to the Construction Committee, to fulfill the previous agreement. After resting until noon on the 1st of this month, Chen returned to Luohe on the original train. It was decided to officially start selling tickets and opening the line to traffic to the Hechao section one month later. The construction has now reached Qiaotouji, 70 li from Hefei. Because Fang Mountain is blocking the way, explosives are being used to blast it away. The opening to Chao may be in the summer of this year.

Special Feature

Personal Views on Revising the Current Trademark Law

Ho Cheuk-Hin's Introduction

Since the Judicial Yuan issued a response to the Executive Yuan in November of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, clarifying that the term "文字" [words] in Article 1, Section 2 of the current Trademark Law [words used in a trademark] [does not include pronunciation] (see Judicial Yuan Consultation No. 1003, published in the 100th issue of the Judicial Yuan Gazette), it has aroused unanimous attention from the whole country. Everyone feels that the current Trademark Law does indeed have many shortcomings in practice. Therefore, revising the current Trademark Law has become a common demand. In the business and industry circles, because of their close relationship with the Trademark Law, several articles have been published successively, such as Chen Xuyuan's "The Necessity of Supplementing the Trademark Law," Hu Xiyuan's "Opinions on the Judicial Yuan's Interpretation of Trademarks," and Pan Yang's "Noteworthy Issues of Trademark Law: Word Form and Pronunciation," etc. (all can be found in major Shanghai newspapers and the special issue on trademark issues of the 97th issue of the Federation of Industry and Commerce Journal). Summarizing their opinions, most of them advocated that the words used in a trademark should include pronunciation. In terms of government agencies, the Trademark Bureau also submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to forward to the Executive Yuan to consult the Judicial Yuan for further interpretation of Article 1, Section 2 of the Trademark Law. The Executive Yuan, at the end of December of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, even automatically consulted the Judicial Yuan for further interpretation of the ambiguities in Article 1, Section 2 of the Trademark Law. As a result, the Judicial Yuan still maintained the previous interpretation without change.

Regarding the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and accountants, in July of the 23rd year, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce felt that the current Trademark Law was quite unsuitable for the industrial and commercial situation, and organized a Trademark Law Research Committee. The selected members were all Shanghai manufacturers' leaders, who gathered to research and propose opinions to the Legislative Yuan for appropriate amendments to the current Trademark Law (see the Shanghai Shen Bao and Shishi Xinbao on July 17th of the 23rd year). This research committee is still constantly holding meetings to discuss issues. On August 13th of the same year, Shanghai accountants Li Wenjie and Qin Yanzhao published an article in the Shanghai Shishi Xinbao expressing their opinions on revising the Trademark Law, proposing six points. Accountant Li has conducted considerable research on the Trademark Law, and their joint opinions are worthy of our attention.

On August 14th of the 23rd year, the Ministry of Industry issued an order to the Trademark Bureau, instructing it to draft a revised draft of the Trademark Law in accordance with the order of the Executive Yuan, and submit it to the Executive Yuan for discussion. The Ministry of Industry specifically ordered the Trademark Bureau to use its case-handling experience to draft a revised draft addressing areas of the Trademark Law that were not yet perfect and submit it for review. After receiving this order, the Trademark Bureau conducted a meticulous study of each article of the Trademark Law, and as a result, listed its opinions and submitted a document to the Ministry on December 12th.

The above is a general overview of the situation after the Judicial Yuan interpreted Article 1, Section 2 of the Trademark Law, in which all parties felt the need to revise the current Trademark Law.

The author feels that due to the evolution of the times, the current Trademark Law inevitably has some aspects that those who formulated the law at that time could not have foreseen. This has not only aroused unanimous attention across the country after the same court interpreted Article 1, Section 2, but even after the government promulgated the Trademark Law in May of the 19th year, many jurists have already made multiple criticisms of it. The structure of Chinese society has its own unique circumstances. This Trademark Law, which is closely related to our country's emerging industry and commerce, should be adapted to the national conditions and the fair conditions of the law in order to become a good law. This is something we cannot help but pay close attention to. Everyone knows that the purpose of formulating the Trademark Law is to protect trademark exclusive rights. However, let us carefully examine whether the current Trademark Law has done its best to protect trademark exclusive rights under the two conditions of adapting to national conditions and complying with legal fairness. I think anyone who pays a little attention will feel that there must be room for discussion. Since there is such a situation, and the law is not an ironclad case once it is promulgated, there is still a way to modify it to remedy it when necessary. The revision of the Trademark Law has become a common demand, as mentioned above. Based on the author's experience in handling trademark cases over the past three years, after the Trademark Bureau officially submitted a document to the Ministry with its opinions on revising the Trademark Law, I will further clarify each point that should be revised or added to the current Trademark Law.

1. Regarding the Issue of Trademark Names

Opening the current Trademark Law, from the first article to the last, there is absolutely no provision regarding trademark names. This shortcoming can only be understood by realizing the importance of trademark names. Every trademark has a name, just as every person has a name. In ordinary general transactions, the buyer only needs to verbally state that they are purchasing goods with a certain trademark name, and the seller will give them goods with that trademark name. Even in large-scale trade, the buyer will definitely state in the order letter or telegram that they are ordering goods with a certain trademark, and there is absolutely no detailed list of the graphic state of the trademark. For example, when buying [White Gold Dragon] trademark cigarettes, the buyer only needs to say [White Gold Dragon], and the shop assistant will naturally sell you the pack or tin of [White Gold Dragon] cigarettes. This proves that the name is an important condition of any trademark and is inseparable from the trademark itself. If there are two or more trademarks with the same name in the same commodity, according to the previous example, there are two or more [White Gold Dragon] trademark cigarettes with the same name, regardless of whether the graphics, symbols, etc. of the trademarks themselves are the same, the seller can freely sell one of the two or more types once the buyer calls out the name. Isn't this kind of malpractice greatly contrary to the purpose of the Trademark Law in protecting trademark exclusive rights? The current Trademark Law has clear provisions on various conditions of the trademark itself, such as words, graphics, symbols, and colors. Why is this other main condition 丨丨name丨丨 ignored, and no protective provisions are added? Although the Trademark Bureau has always prohibited the subsequent registration of trademarks with the same name, after all, the current Trademark Law does not stipulate this clearly, and it is inevitable to feel that there is no legal basis for doing so. Article 1, Section 2 of the current Trademark Law stipulates all the conditions of the trademark itself. I propose to add a provision regarding trademark names in the same article and section. Then, the original provision should be changed to [The words, graphics, symbols, or their combination used in the trademark must be particularly prominent, and specify the name and the colors applied].

2. Regarding the Issue of Trademark Word Pronunciation

Although the Judicial Yuan's interpretation of the words used in a trademark stipulated in Article 1, Section 2 of the Trademark Law as [not including pronunciation] has aroused countless criticisms, once the law is interpreted by the statutory authority, it should be implemented according to its interpretation. Therefore, we do not need to discuss this interpretation of the Judicial Yuan any further. However, from the perspective of the legislative purpose of the Trademark Law, if the words used in a trademark do not include pronunciation, then unscrupulous people will take advantage of the loopholes in the regulations, try their best to use words with the same pronunciation as the words used in registered trademarks as trademarks, and carry out disguised imitation. This is greatly contrary to the legislative purpose of protecting trademark exclusive rights. First, as I have said above, in ordinary general transactions, the buyer only needs to verbally say that they are buying goods with a certain trademark, and the seller can sell it to them accordingly. Therefore, I advocate that clear provisions should be added to trademark names. Trademarks with the same name are certainly sufficient to cause mistaken purchases, but trademarks with the same pronunciation can also cause confusion in transactions. This is with regard to trademark names. The words used in trademarks should include pronunciation. Second, many trademarks, especially Western medicine trademarks, are composed of only two or three words, such as [Lysol Machine], [Guoneng Cling]. These types of trademarks only constitute a very simple concept in the minds of buyers. In other words, buyers can only recall those few words in their minds. If the words used in the trademark do not include pronunciation, there will inevitably be word trademarks with the same pronunciation in the same commodity. Since the law cannot prohibit them, buyers will inevitably be at a loss and make mistaken purchases. This is with regard to word trademarks. The words used in trademarks should also include pronunciation. In addition, assuming that there are two trademarks in the same commodity, one is called [Bat Deer Brand] and the other is called [Fu Lu Brand], I dare to say that buyers will definitely make mistaken purchases because in ordinary general transactions, the seller gives the goods based on the buyer's verbal call. Also, assuming that there are two word trademarks in the same commodity, one is wrigley and the other is rwgly, I am also convinced that the coexistence of these two trademarks will definitely cause confusion in transactions because many buyers often only remember the pronunciation of the words. In summary, the malpractice of confusion in the pronunciation of trademark words is no less than the similarity of graphics, symbols, etc. The Trademark Bureau has always only allowed one of the word trademarks with confusing pronunciations, such as [Yin Dan Shi Lin] and [Yin Tang Shi Ling], [Wei Jing] and [Wei Jin], or trademarks with the same name, such as [Fish Head] and [Jade Hand], stacombaa and suckomb, to be registered for exclusive use. I believe that this approach is very consistent with the legislative purpose of the Trademark Law in protecting trademark exclusive rights. However, since the Judicial Yuan's interpretation case does not allow us not to comply, in order to remedy the various malpractices caused by not considering the pronunciation of trademark words, I propose to add a clause after Article 1, Section 2 of the current Trademark Law. The clause is [The words used in the trademark include pronunciation, based on the national pronunciation of each country]. (To be continued)

Local News

Italian Ambassador to China, Vincenzo Arangio Ruiz, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon

Various Circles in China and Italy Welcomed Him, Resting Briefly in Shanghai Before Proceeding to Beijing

The newly appointed first Italian Ambassador to China, Vincenzo Arangio Ruiz, along with his family members and aviation entourage, arrived in Shanghai on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso at 2:30 PM yesterday. Mayor Wu and representatives from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, as well as the Italian Minister, went to welcome him. Details are as follows:

Chinese and Foreign Welcome

Those who went to the pier to welcome him yesterday afternoon included Secretary Geng Jiaqi, representing Mayor Wu Tiecheng; Zhao Tiezhang, representative of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs; Italian Minister to China, Barone Alberto Paulucci di Calboli; Counselor An Fusuo; Aviation Attaché Raul di Lauro; Consul General Nalloni; the Ambassador's Private Secretary, Gabbazzo; and Baron Saidi. Also present were Commander Raimondi of the Italian warship Lepanto, Commander Gregorio, and a small team of Italian sailors from the ship, about twenty or so people, who went to the pier to welcome him.

Arrival Situation

The Conte Rosso ship, on which the Ambassador was traveling, was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai around 11:00 AM yesterday. However, due to fog encountered en route, it was delayed until 2:30 PM before arriving at the port and docking at the Gonghexiang Wharf on East Broadway Road in Hongkou. After the Ambassador arrived, he met with the welcoming party on the ship and was introduced to each of them by the Italian Minister to China, Barone Alberto Paulucci di Calboli. He then disembarked with his wife and others at 3:00 PM and immediately returned to his new residence on Yuyuan Road to rest.

Ambassador's Remarks

The newly appointed Italian Ambassador, Vincenzo Arangio Ruiz, dressed in a dark blue ordinary suit, interacted with the welcoming personnel with an unusually amiable attitude. According to what he told our reporter during a brief meeting, he was very interested in his first trip to China. He would stay in Shanghai for a few days to rest before proceeding to Beijing. The date for presenting his credentials has not yet been decided. After presenting his credentials in Beijing, he will return to Shanghai, and at that time, he would be very willing to talk with everyone in detail. Regarding Sino-Italian relations, he stated that the friendly relations have always been cordial, and in the future, he would be willing to make great efforts to jointly promote them.

Accompanying Personnel

Those who came with the Ambassador included his private secretaries, Baron Saidi and Gabbazzo, who had arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. Those who arrived in Shanghai on the same ship as the Ambassador yesterday afternoon included Ambassadorial officer Marelli, aviation entourage Colonel Delego, and Mr. Ruiz's wife, daughter, and two sons. In addition, there were five male and female attendants, totaling more than ten people.

No Social Engagements for Now

After the Ambassador arrived in Shanghai, a telegram has been sent to Nanjing by the Foreign Affairs Office to report his arrival and request instructions on the date of entry into Beijing. It can be decided after receiving the reply. Before entering Beijing, Mr. Ruiz will not have any formal social engagements before presenting his credentials, except for attending a banquet hosted by Italian Minister Barone Alberto Paulucci di Calboli at 7:30 PM last night.

Italian Ambassador Vincenzo Arangio Ruiz and his wife (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Minister to Belgium, Zhang Naiyan, Returned to China Yesterday

Unwilling to Express Anything to the Press

Our country's Minister to Belgium, Zhang Naiyan, returned to China on summons and arrived in Shanghai on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso at 2:30 PM yesterday. The ship docked at the Gonghexiang Wharf. Zhao Tiezhang, Section Chief of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and friends of Mr. Zhang, went to the port to welcome him. After disembarking, Mr. Zhang went straight to his private residence on Daxilu Road to rest. Mr. Zhang did not want to express anything to the press, only saying that he was on leave for three months and would go to Beijing that evening or the next to pay his respects to Foreign Minister Wang and report on his experiences abroad. While abroad, Minister Zhang was not only responsible for handling diplomatic negotiations, but also for investigating construction projects in various countries on behalf of the Construction Committee, resulting in physical exhaustion. This time, he requested leave to return to China, partly to report on the diplomatic situation and the results of his investigations, and partly to recover from his accumulated fatigue. According to what Minister Zhang told visitors yesterday, the situation of the European powers is currently extremely tense, but there is still considerable understanding between France and Germany. Although the situation in Southern European countries is extremely complicated, it is unlikely to lead to conflict for the time being. Moreover, since the Great War, the people's aversion to war has not diminished in the slightest. There will probably be no war in 1935. Before leaving Europe, Mr. Zhang personally went to various European countries to conduct on-site investigations. The number of unemployed people in various countries is decreasing day by day, and they are all able to live and work in peace. This is because the government promotes production and construction to solve the people's livelihood problems. Confucius said, "Enrich them, then teach them." Guanzi said, "When the granary is full, then they know etiquette and righteousness; when they have enough food and clothing, then they know honor and shame." Therefore, our country's fundamental plan is to concentrate its efforts on developing production and construction to solve the people's livelihood problems. As for Sino-Belgian relations, they are exceptionally cordial. Our country has about two hundred students studying abroad, all of whom are able to be pragmatic and strive to learn, and are expected to be promising young people in the future. It is heard that Mr. Zhang will soon go to Beijing to meet with Foreign Minister Wang and report on the diplomatic situation, as well as make a statement to Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the National Government Construction Committee.

Minister Zhang Naiyan (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Shen Yi Returned to China Yesterday and Arrived in Shanghai

Returned from Attending the International Road Conference, Gave a Written Statement on the Ship Yesterday

Mr. Shen Yi, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, was ordered to go to Germany in June last year to attend the Seventh International Road Conference and participate in the Yellow River Experiment hosted by Professor Engels of Germany. He completed his official duties last month and returned to China on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso. He arrived in Shanghai at 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon. Those who went to welcome him included Mr. Li Dachao, Section Chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government; Xu Yuanfang, Director of the Two Roads General Affairs Office; Mo Heng, Director of the Materials Office; Zheng Baocheng, Section Chief of the Third Section of the Municipal Utilities Bureau; Xue Cixin, Qiu Xieyun, Xiao Qingyun, Xu Guansan, Tan Wenqing, senior officials of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, and many of his relatives and friends. After disembarking, Mr. Shen went straight to his private residence to rest. Mr. Shen is scheduled to return to work within a few days and report everything to the government and the National Economic Council. In addition to Mrs. Shen, Mr. Zhou Fengjiu and Mr. Tong Enjiong, representatives of our country who attended the road conference, also returned to China with Mr. Shen.

Mr. Shen gave a written statement on the ship yesterday, saying: "I was ordered by the government in early June last year to go to Germany to attend the Seventh International Road Conference, and was entrusted by the National Economic Council and the Yellow River Conservancy Commission to participate in the Yellow River Experiment hosted by Professor Engels of Germany. It has been seven months now. A total of six representatives from our country attended the road conference. The government representatives were originally Chen Ticheng and myself. Later, Mr. Chen was unable to go due to official business, and Zhao Zukang took his place. In addition, there were Mr. Zhou Fengjiu and Mr. Tong Enjiong, representatives of the Hunan Provincial Government, and Mr. Wang Nanyuan, a representative of the Anhui Provincial Government, and Mr. Jiang Hong, a representative of the China National Road Construction Association. The conference opened in Munich, Germany on September 3 last year and closed in Berlin on the 18th. Representatives from 49 countries attended, with a total of more than 2,000 people. There were six items on the agenda, including asphalt roads, cement roads, the most economical road construction methods, traffic management, transportation, and safety issues. Several months before the conference, the International Road Association distributed the above-mentioned agenda items to each member country, and the association prepared a general report based on the reports of each country. The task of the conference was to discuss this general report, with no other proposals or texts for discussion. This is different from general conferences. The report of our country this time was compiled and sent by the National Economic Council after the relevant parties provided materials in advance. Not only was it consistent with the form of other countries, but also its content was not inferior. Therefore, it has received much attention from the representatives of various countries. This road conference is held every four years. The next, that is, the eighth conference, will be held in the Netherlands in 1938. The location of the ninth conference is approximately in Hungary. The locations of the subsequent conferences have not yet been determined. When the conference closed in Berlin this time, I, in my capacity as the leader of the Chinese delegation, made a speech, revealing my hope that we could have a conference in our country in the future so that people from all countries could truly recognize the new China that is struggling for peace. I deeply hope that during this period, the country will become more unified day by day and gradually embark on the road of production and construction, and with the doubled efforts of engineers across the country, it will not be difficult to have better results in ten years to meet the world, and it is not impossible to have the day when the conference is held in our country. The biggest feeling of this trip is that, looking at all countries, there is a comprehensive plan and a certain policy for road construction. Even some countries, because they do not produce asphalt in their country, would rather give up asphalt roads than build them. This kind of spirit is very worthy of emulation. Of our six people, in addition to Zhou Fengjiu and Tong Enjiong, who returned to China on the same boat as me, Zhao Zukang returned to China via the Americas. Wang Nanyuan and Jiang Hong were originally studying in Germany and are still in Germany. Regarding the Yellow River Experiment, I will submit a detailed written report to the National Economic Council. This experiment is a continuation of the previous two years' experiments. It started in the mountains of southern Germany in June last year and was completed in mid-November. The experiment was divided into four groups, and its purpose was to study the impact of wide levees and narrow levees on the Yellow River. The results are very satisfactory. I also took advantage of the opportunity to participate in the experiment in Germany to exchange views on the river management issue with Professor Engels from time to time. As a result, it was found that Mr. Engels's proposition is actually the same principle as the river management method of Pan Jixun of the Ming Dynasty in our country, which communicates with each other, and it is also an unexpected gain of my trip. In addition to attending the road conference and participating in the Yellow River Experiment in Germany, I also visited the United Kingdom, France, Russia, Italy, Switzerland, the Netherlands, the Czech Republic, and other countries with my wife, and I had a brief investigation on the water conservancy, municipal administration, and engineering education of each country. In addition to the investigation along the way, I have many feelings. In a nutshell, everyone is actively preparing for war."

He attended the expanded memorial week at the Municipal Government yesterday morning and completed the inauguration oath ceremony. Details are as follows:

Participating Personnel

Those who participated in the ceremony included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director Wen Chaoji of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Secretary General Yu Hongjun of the Municipal Government, Director Li Tingan of the Health Bureau, Commissioners Wang Changchun and Luo Panhui, Secretaries Guo Shen, Geng Jiaqi, and Tang Shixuan, all staff of the Municipal Government, directors of various sub-bureaus of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, directors of various police stations, and guests Dong Chongshan, a representative of the High Court Second Branch; Shen Xiqing, President of the Local Court; Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs; Zeng Yiding, Commander of the Second Fleet of the Navy; Ye Baoqi, Battalion Commander of the Guard Battalion; Pu Cheng, Staff Officer; Zhu Shaoping, Deputy Director of the Municipal Gazetteer, and over a hundred other people.

Oath of Office

At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the meeting was opened with a bell. All participants gathered in the auditorium. The Municipal Public Security Bureau also sent a military band to play music on the spot. Mayor Wu presided over the ceremony, and after performing the ritual, Mayor Wu gave a speech first, then Mayor Wu presided over the oath, Director Wen read the oath, and gave a reply, and then announced the completion of the ceremony and dismissal of the meeting. After the meeting, Secretary General Yu, Director Li, President Shen, and senior officials of the Municipal Government all shook hands with Director Wen to congratulate him.

Mayor's Speech

National construction can be roughly divided into two types: political and economic. Whether it is political or economic construction, it is for the purpose of benefiting the people. If we want to succeed in economic construction, we should first work hard on political construction, because political construction is the driving force and engine of all construction. The most important thing in political construction is public security. Those of us who take the promotion of municipal construction as our duty want to enable the development of local undertakings and the people to sincerely help the government, then handling public security is even more important, because if public security is handled perfectly, the people will be able to live and work in peace, and all construction can be carried out actively. And the public security undertaking especially depends on whether the police can achieve effective results. If we want the police to achieve good results, we should lead by example, abide by the law, and take the protection of national rights and the interests of the people as our duty. Shanghai is an economic center, the gateway to the capital, and also a large international city. Therefore, those who come to China for sightseeing must first come to Shanghai, and the results of the police are the most obvious. Therefore, the management of the police should not be neglected in the slightest. I hope that Director Wen understands the importance of his responsibility, should never forget his duties, be able to abide by the laws and decrees of the country, obey the orders of his superiors, and take the protection of the interests of the people as important."

Mr. Wen's Reply

Director Wen's reply briefly stated: "Being ordered to serve as the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau of this city, I deeply know that the responsibility is heavy, and I should work hard for the public to avoid failing. In the future, I should be more self-motivated,恪遵Mayor's guidance, obey the orders of the government, and lead my subordinates to maintain the security of Shanghai, so as to promote the progress of the police administration in this city. I am especially grateful to the guests who have come to the scene."

Bureau Chief's Oath
